1281

1282 <h1 class="entry-title">

1283What Are Trichomes and How Do They Affect Marijuana?</h1>

1284

1285 </div>

1286

1287 <div class="et_pb_title_featured_container">

1288<span class="et_pb_image_wrap">

1289<img loading="lazy" width="1200" height="500" src="https://medicalmarijuanainc.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/iStock-543350422-1.jpg" alt="marijuana trichomes" title="Closeup of Marijuana Trichomes" srcset="https://medicalmarijuanainc.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/iStock-543350422-1.jpg 1200w, https://medicalmarijuanainc.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/iStock-543350422-1-300x125.jpg 300w, https://medicalmarijuanainc.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/iStock-543350422-1-768x320.jpg 768w, https://medicalmarijuanainc.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/iStock-543350422-1-1024x427.jpg 1024w, https://medicalmarijuanainc.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/iStock-543350422-1-750x313.jpg 750w" sizes="(max-width: 1200px) 100vw, 1200px" class="wp-image-29999" />

1290</span>

1291</div>

1292

1293 </div>

1294<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_post_content et_pb_post_content_0_tb_body">

1295

1296

1297

1298 <h3>

1299<i>

1300<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1301Those tiny, shiny bulbs that appear on your marijuana contain most of the plants cannabinoids and other active compounds that provide marijuana&#8217;s scents, flavors, and effects.</span>

1302</i>

1303</h3>

1304

1305<p>

1306<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1307Take a close look at marijuana plants and youll notice shiny and sticky crystals that blanket the plants leaves and buds. These are trichomes &#8212; tiny microscopic outgrowths that contain the cannabis plant&#8217;s essential oils and the cannabinoids, terpenes, and flavonoids that make your</span>

1308<a href="https://medicalmarijuanainc.com/">

1309<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1310medical marijuana</span>

1311</a>

1312<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1313 therapeutically beneficial and give recreational marijuana its flavor and potency.</span>

1314</p>

1315

1316<p>

1317<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1318Here we take a look at trichomes, their natural purpose, and how they play a key role in the characteristics and effects of marijuana.</span>

1319</p>

1320

1321<h2>

1322<b>

1323What are Trichomes?</b>

1324</h2>

1325

1326<p>

1327<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1328Trichomes are small resin glands found on marijuana flowers, leaves, and in lower numbers, stalks. Originating from the Greek word Trchma, meaning growth of hair, trichomes viewed under a magnifying glass look like tiny hairs with a round, bulbous head at their tips. To the naked eye, these resin glands, which range in width from 10 to 100 micrometers, look like shiny, sticky crystals, giving buds their frosty appearance. </span>

1329</p>

1330

1331<p>

1332<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1333Trichomes begin to appear on marijuana as soon as the plants enter their</span>

1334<a href="https://medicalmarijuanainc.com/care-growing-cannabis-flowering-process/">

1335<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1336flowering stage</span>

1337</a>

1338<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1339, toward the end of the lifecycle and just before the buds are ready for harvest. As the plants buds begin to appear, trichomes also start to form along the stalk, the leaves, and the buds. Growers need to be careful when handling marijuana plants during the flowering stage, as trichomes are volatile and can be degraded by physical contact, as well as heat, light, and oxygen.</span>

1340</p>

1341

1342<p>

1343<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1344Because they are filled with resin, when trichomes break, they release the sticky oil inside. This is what gives some marijuana buds their stickiness. The more trichomes there are, the more resin they will release when handled roughly.</span>

1345</p>

1346

1347<p>

1348<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1349While trichomes offer multiple benefits to the marijuana plant, to marijuana consumers theyre primarily appreciated because they hold the compounds that are responsible for cannabis effects, as well as the way it smells and tastes.</span>

1350</p>

1351

1352<h2>

1353<b>

1354What is the Function of Trichomes?</b>

1355</h2>

1356

1357<p>

1358<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1359Trichomes arent limited to marijuana plants. Rather, the production of trichomes can be observed in many species of plants, taking on various physical forms. Trichomes help keep plants of all kinds safe, healthy, and productive.</span>

1360</p>

1361

1362<p>

1363<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1364On cannabis plants, trichomes serve as defenders against insects, animals, and other non-living environmental variables that may harm the plant. When female marijuana plants begin producing buds, they become especially vulnerable to pests. Ants, mites, caterpillars, and moths are just some of the bugs that may ruin your plants buds and damage its health.</span>

1365</p>

1366

1367<p>

1368<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1369With their strong aroma and bitter taste, trichomes help deter animals and bugs. They also help protect the plants from potentially harmful UV rays and damaging winds.</span>

1370</p>

1371

1372<p>

1373<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1374If youre </span>

1375<a href="https://medicalmarijuanainc.com/grow-weed-home/">

1376<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1377growing your own marijuana</span>

1378</a>

1379<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1380, trichomes can help you know when your flowers are ready for harvest. When trichomes are clear, the plants are not yet fully mature. Once the trichome stalks appear cloudy and opaque or turn a red or amber color, depending on the strain, you can expect that the flowers have developed or are close to developing an ideal cannabinoid profile.</span>

1381</p>

1382

1383<p>

1384<img loading="lazy" class="alignnone wp-image-30107 size-large" src="https://www.medicalmarijuanainc.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/iStock-626429256-1-1024x427.jpg" alt="marijuana trichomes" width="640" height="267" srcset="https://medicalmarijuanainc.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/iStock-626429256-1-1024x427.jpg 1024w, https://medicalmarijuanainc.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/iStock-626429256-1-300x125.jpg 300w, https://medicalmarijuanainc.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/iStock-626429256-1-768x320.jpg 768w, https://medicalmarijuanainc.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/iStock-626429256-1-750x313.jpg 750w, https://medicalmarijuanainc.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/iStock-626429256-1.jpg 1200w" sizes="(max-width: 640px) 100vw, 640px" />

1385</p>

1386

1387<h2>

1388<b>

1389Why are Trichomes Important to Marijuana?</b>

1390</h2>

1391

1392<p>

1393<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1394While the entire marijuana plant contains cannabinoids, it&#8217;s within the plants trichomes that the active compounds are most highly concentrated. As plants start to bloom and trichomes grow on the marijuana plant, cannabinoid synthesis begins within the trichomes, as cells become the precursors to the over 100 cannabinoids the plant produces.</span>

1395</p>

1396

1397<p>

1398<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1399Compared to the rest of the marijuana plant, trichomes contain a much higher concentration of:</span>

1400</p>

1401

1402<ul>

1403

1404<li style="font-weight: 400;">

1405<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1406Cannabinoids</span>

1407</li>

1408

1409<li style="font-weight: 400;">

1410<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1411Terpenes</span>

1412</li>

1413

1414<li style="font-weight: 400;">

1415<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1416 Flavonoids</span>

1417</li>

1418

1419</ul>

1420

1421<p>

1422<i>

1423<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1424Cannabinoids</span>

1425</i>

1426</p>

1427

1428<p>

1429<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1430Marijuana contains more than 100 so-far identified cannabinoids, including the well-known compounds tetrahydrocannabinol (THC), the intoxicating compound that elicits euphoric effects, and cannabidiol (</span>

1431<a href="https://medicalmarijuanainc.com/what-is-cbd-oil/">

1432<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1433CBD</span>

1434</a>

1435<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1436). These cannabinoids interact with your bodys native</span>

1437 <a href="https://medicalmarijuanainc.com/endocannabinoid-system/">

1438<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1439endocannabinoid system</span>

1440</a>

1441<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1442, a regulatory network that keeps many of your functions in homeostasis.</span>

1443</p>

1444

1445<p>

1446<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1447Sharing a similar chemical makeup as the endocannabinoids that are synthesized naturally by the body, cannabis-derived cannabinoids are able to interact with the endocannabinoid systems cannabinoid receptors to stimulate the chemical reactions to produce natural beneficial effects.</span>

1448</p>

1449

1450<p>

1451<i>

1452<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1453Terpenes</span>

1454</i>

1455</p>

1456

1457<p>

1458<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1459Responsible for giving marijuana flowers their flavor and aromatic diversity,</span>

1460 <a href="https://medicalmarijuanainc.com/terpenes-terpenoids-matter/">

1461<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1462terpenes</span>

1463</a>

1464<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1465 have also shown to</span>

1466 <a href="https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pmc/articles/PMC3165946/">

1467<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1468work with cannabinoids</span>

1469</a>

1470<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1471 to enhance their natural balancing properties in whats called the </span>

1472<a href="https://medicalmarijuanainc.com/can-hemp-oil-provide-entourage-effect/">

1473<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1474entourage effect</span>

1475</a>

1476<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1477. Like cannabinoids, terpenes bind to receptors to stimulate</span>

1478 <a href="http://www.tandfonline.com/doi/abs/10.1300/J175v01n03_08">

1479<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1480wide-ranging effects</span>

1481</a>

1482<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1483, and alter the release of neurotransmitters like dopamine and serotonin.</span>

1484</p>

1485

1486<p>

1487<i>

1488<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1489Flavonoids</span>

1490</i>

1491</p>

1492

1493<p>

1494<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1495Flavonoids are phytonutrients that contribute to the plants color, taste, and smell. They also work together with the other compounds to encourage a wide variety of health benefits. Flavonoids unique to cannabis are called cannaflavins, and</span>

1496<a href="https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pubmed/3754224">

1497 <span style="font-weight: 400;">

1498research</span>

1499</a>

1500<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1501 has already discovered that they offer some</span>

1502 <a href="https://www.sciencedirect.com/science/article/pii/0006295285903259?via%3Dihub">

1503<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1504promising properties</span>

1505</a>

1506<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1507.</span>

1508</p>

1509

1510<h2>

1511<b>

1512What are the Different Types of Trichomes?</b>

1513</h2>

1514

1515<p>

1516<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1517On the marijuana plant, there are three types of trichomes:</span>

1518</p>

1519

1520<ul>

1521

1522<li style="font-weight: 400;">

1523<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1524Bulbous</span>

1525</li>

1526

1527<li style="font-weight: 400;">

1528<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1529Capitate-sessile</span>

1530</li>

1531

1532<li style="font-weight: 400;">

1533<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1534Capitate-stalked</span>

1535</li>

1536

1537</ul>

1538

1539<p>

1540<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1541Bulbous trichomes are the smallest of the three types, nearly invisible to the naked eye. They appear on the surface of the entire plant, and are as small as 10-15 micrometers. While bulbous trichomes do contain cannabinoids and other compounds, their tiny size limits their capacity.</span>

1542</p>

1543

1544<p>

1545<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1546Slightly larger and more common, capitate-sessile trichomes contain a small stalk and head that is more abundant in cannabinoids compared to the bulbous type.</span>

1547</p>

1548

1549<p>

1550<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1551Ranging anywhere between 50-100 micrometers wide, capitate-stalked trichomes are the largest variety of the resin glands, and in general the type that youll likely notice when looking at your medical marijuana plants. They feature a prominent stalk and large gland head that serves as the focal point for most of the cannabinoids and other beneficial compounds.</span>

1552</p>

1553

1554<p>

1555<img loading="lazy" class="alignnone wp-image-30108 size-large" src="https://www.medicalmarijuanainc.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/2-2-1024x427.jpg" alt="THC trichomes" width="640" height="267" srcset="https://medicalmarijuanainc.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/2-2-1024x427.jpg 1024w, https://medicalmarijuanainc.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/2-2-300x125.jpg 300w, https://medicalmarijuanainc.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/2-2-768x320.jpg 768w, https://medicalmarijuanainc.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/2-2-750x313.jpg 750w, https://medicalmarijuanainc.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/2-2.jpg 1200w" sizes="(max-width: 640px) 100vw, 640px" />

1556</p>

1557

1558<h2>

1559<b>

1560Trichomes: The Source of Kief and Hash</b>

1561</h2>

1562

1563<p>

1564<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1565Marijuana users interested in increasing their cannabinoid intake can harvest trichomes and use them to produce the kief or hash. By containing only trichome heads, the two concentrates offer the highest potency of nearly all marijuana products.</span>

1566</p>

1567

1568<p>

1569<a href="https://medicalmarijuanainc.com/what-is-kief-and-why-is-it-so-popular/">

1570<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1571Kief</span>

1572</a>

1573<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1574 is the accumulation of trichomes in the form of a shimmery powder. Typically, a three-chamber herb grinder is used to separate the kief from the flower, producing a highly-potent concentrate that can be inhaled by smoking or vaping, or added to foods and beverages.</span>

1575</p>

1576

1577<p>

1578<a href="https://medicalmarijuanainc.com/lets-hash-beginners-guide-hash/">

1579<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1580Hash</span>

1581</a>

1582<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1583 is similar to kief, except that the trichomes are pressed into a solid mass. Most commonly made by separating the flowers trichomes from the plant by hand or dry-sifting with a screen, hash can be inhaled via smoking, vaping, or dabbing, or infused into</span>

1584 <a href="https://medicalmarijuanainc.com/beginners-guide-marijuana-edibles/">

1585<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1586marijuana edibles</span>

1587</a>

1588<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1589.</span>

1590</p>

1591

1592<p>

1593The leaves growing nearest the marijuana plant&#8217;s buds are typically covered in trichomes as well, giving them a frosty appearance and earning them the name <em>

1594sugar leaves</em>

1595. These leaves are often saved during trimming for use in making cannabis oils or edibles. Read more about <a href="https://medicalmarijuanainc.com/cannabis-leaves-and-their-uses/">

1596cannabis leaves</a>

1597.</p>

1598

1599<p>

1600<img loading="lazy" class="alignnone wp-image-30109 size-large" src="https://www.medicalmarijuanainc.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/5-2-1-1024x427.jpg" alt="trichomes color" width="640" height="267" srcset="https://medicalmarijuanainc.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/5-2-1-1024x427.jpg 1024w, https://medicalmarijuanainc.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/5-2-1-300x125.jpg 300w, https://medicalmarijuanainc.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/5-2-1-768x320.jpg 768w, https://medicalmarijuanainc.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/5-2-1-750x313.jpg 750w, https://medicalmarijuanainc.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/5-2-1.jpg 1200w" sizes="(max-width: 640px) 100vw, 640px" />

1601</p>

1602

1603<h2>

1604<b>

1605Learn More about Medical Marijuana</b>

1606</h2>

1607

1608<p>

1609<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1610Marijuana is <a href="https://medicalmarijuanainc.com/where-is-marijuana-legal/">

1611now legal</a>

1612 in some capacity in more than half of U.S. states, with</span>

1613 <span style="font-weight: 400;">

161433 states</span>

1615<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1616 permitting the use of marijuana for medical purposes and 11 legalizing recreational use. As a result, more people are interested in learning how to grow and harvest their own marijuana.</span>

1617</p>

1618

1619<p>

1620<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1621You can learn even more about growing and handling marijuana by visiting our</span>

1622 <a href="https://medicalmarijuanainc.com/">

1623<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1624Cannabis 101 page</span>

1625</a>

1626<span style="font-weight: 400;">

1627.</span>

1628</p>

1629
